Cases\n69: \n70: 1. **Config Change**: User updates a VirtualService. Pilot triggers a push, builds a new `PushContext`, and generates new xDS resources for affected Envoys.\n71: 2. **Endpoint Update**: Kubernetes endpoint changes. Pilot updates the service registry, builds a new `PushContext`, and pushes updated endpoints to Envoy.\n72: \n73: ## Best Practices\n74: \n75: - Always use the current `PushContext` for xDS generation to ensure consistency.\n76: - Avoid mutating `PushContext` after construction; treat it as immutable.\n77: - Use `PushContext` methods to access mesh state (services, virtual services, etc.) instead of accessing raw data.\n78: - Profile and optimize `PushContext` construction for large meshes.\n79: \n80: ## Related Components\n81: ","endLine":81,"startLine":61}],"file":".github/.copilot/domain_knowledge/pilot_push_context.md","repo":"github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae","type":"file","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae/-/blob/.github/.copilot/domain_knowledge/pilot_push_context.md"}]}}}
